Grain: Bulls Lower Prices to Sell 156

Spot Flour Weakens

Yesterday, the spot flour market suddenly showed a weak and unsustainable appearance. Due to the inactivity of actual sales in the North, and stagnation in Guangfu, the existing goods about 500,000 to 600,000 bags, are moving. A small number of bulls could not wait and sold at bargain prices. However, there was little interest from buyers, so the price dropped significantly, by about two fen compared to the previous day. There is currently no difference between April and May spot goods. The opening price for May goods ranged from 8.5 fen to as low as 7.5 fen. However, goods from factories that are unavailable in the market are still priced high, such as Maigenxu at 1 qian net, and Shuangma at 9 fen net. Fuxin factory goods are still offered at 2 liang, 1 qian and 5 fen discounted, and they insist on that price.

Rice Market in Hexia Flat and Weak 157

South Shanghai: Yesterday, there were more than 20 sources from various merchants. Due to bad weather, there were not many buyers at local stores. Thick Japonica rice was stable, and some thin Indica rice arrived. The market was congested, and the outgoing goods on this street, top-grade rice, moved slightly. There was little demand for foreign Dujian rice, and the opening price was 2 jiao lower. Early rice and Yin Yuan rice arrived and sold at a balanced rate. The market did not fluctuate.

North Shanghai: Yesterday, the rice market was sluggish. Shops lining the market were relatively active, but turnover was limited, making it difficult to stabilize sales. There was a tendency to lower prices. There were few Changshu and Xishui goods arriving, and prices stabilized. Early and late rice, as well as the selling of altered Yin Yuan rice, were dull, with prices slightly down by a jiao. Not many foreign Dujian rice arrived, and the opening price remained stable.

Sales of Foreign Rice Continue to be Strong 158

Yesterday, the foreign rice market temporarily stabilized. Due to the fact that the passports led by the Jiangbei gang have not yet been issued, there is no large selling group. However, in order to expand sales channels, foreign merchants allow foreign rice shipped to other ports to be handled according to the bank mortgage method, and the payment can be collected in the sales location. This aroused the consultants of the foreign gang, and the appetite of the users on our street and the hoarders was particularly good, so the market was strong and the high-priced goods were able to recover their prices. The general office opened 5,000 packages of Small Jiao rice, priced at 10 yuan, 1 jiao and 8 fen to 9 yuan and 8 jiao and 7 fen, 2,500 packages of No. 1 Saigon rice, priced at 11 yuan, 3 jiao and a half to 11 yuan and 1 jiao, and 200 packages of Mindang rice, priced at 10 yuan and 3 jiao. Except for 2,000 packages of Small Jiao handled by the Yangtze River gang, they were all received by the households on our street. The futures opening of Small Jiao in May was 250 tons, priced at 5 liang, and No. 1 Saigon in May was 300 tons, priced at 5 liang and 2 qian and a half. The market price was also similar to the previous day.

Silk and Tea Are Temporarily Stable, Silkworm Rearing is Unsuccessful 159

Purely Affected by Rain and Cold in Spring

Third Sleep Delayed

Linping in Zhejiang and Hangzhou has always been a famous silkworm rearing area. This year, due to economic reasons, the number of silkworm eggs raised has been greatly reduced, only accounting for 40% of previous years. After the eggs were hatched, the development was quite good. The early batch was about to enter the third sleep, and the late batch was also consuming leaves well in the second sleep. However, in recent days, it has been rainy and not sunny, and the weather has been very cold, causing the silkworms that have eaten enough leaves in the second sleep to delay their third sleep. The silkworms that were consuming leaves well are also eating less, and buyers are using fire to supplement heat.

Foreign Merchants' Silk Market Increasingly Lifeless 160

Yesterday, the foreign merchants' silk market in this port was increasingly lifeless. The New York telegram turned white, and the price for B-grade material was still less than 500 liang. Factories had difficulty selling at a loss. Silk sales in England and France were still quiet. Yesterday, only Boxin imported 6 packages of Huang Yao Warp silk, Xiangji imported 10 packages of Huang Coarse silk, and Kechang imported 16 packages of Huang silk. Prices were generally flat and weak.

A Large Batch of Woolen Cloth Imports Next Month 161

Recently, sales of woolen cloth have been low, with few large transactions, and prices have been declining. The poor market sentiment is rare in recent years. Both buyers and sellers feel difficult, and most brokers have stopped trading. However, imported goods continue to arrive, mostly goods temporarily stored in Hong Kong last time. It is heard that a large batch of goods will arrive next month, because since the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the woolen cloth industry has cancelled orders from foreign firms. Yesterday, the guild received a letter from the Foreign Merchants' Import Association, stating that the situation is peaceful and the goods must be loaded. The guild replied that if the situation is peaceful and the goods can flow smoothly, we will agree. Now, we have received another letter from the association, stating that the situation is largely restored to normal, and the goods must be loaded now, and it will take 42 days to arrive in port. There is no reason to postpone it again, please inform all members. It is expected that a large batch of several thousand boxes of woolen cloth will be imported next month.

Jubao Basin Zhigong Serge Reduced by 2 Qian and Stabilized 162

Jubao Basin Yuanqing Zhigong Serge is exclusively distributed by British Anli Foreign Firm. It has had strong sales over the years and is a well-known brand of Zhigong serge. There is a joint brand contract among traders, so the selling price is unified. The highest selling price in previous years was 7 liang, and the lowest was 6 liang and 5 qian. This spring, the opening price was also 6 liang and 5 qian. Due to slow sales in the market and falling prices of various goods, traders decided yesterday to reduce the price by 2.5 qian per yard, and the wholesale price is only 6 liang and 2.5 qian per yard. If selling original box to brokers for resale, some commissions can be deducted at their discretion.

Glimpses of Zhabei 164

— Jin

Since Zhabei experienced severe artillery fire, the good residents have all fled, and the houses and huts have become rubble, creating a desolate scene of wailing and howling, almost an uninhabited area.

Consequently, Zhao Xinbo of Zhabei, Zheng Xiaoxu of Zhabei, and others, relying on false pretenses and leveraging each other's influence, organized things like "Pseudo Local Maintenance Committees." These rebellious bandits will naturally be sanctioned by national laws, which I won't concern myself with.

Now, the Japanese are also using Koreans to colonize Zhabei. On one hand, Koreans from Dalian and Qingdao, instructed by the Japanese authorities, are forming commercial inspection groups to inspect Zhabei. On the other hand, three groups of Korean prostitutes are being moved from Qingdao to provide entertainment for the Japanese soldiers. Looking at it this way, what kind of phenomenon does the world of Zhabei present? Righteous Chinese people would never want to live in Zhabei, nor would they want to see such a situation. Although there is talk of a turning point in the ceasefire negotiations, and the drafting committee started yesterday, I don't believe there will be any results. The ceasefire negotiations have been going on for a long time; one day they say this, the next day they say that. What value does such a conference have?

In short, until the Japanese soldiers have completely withdrawn, not only Zhabei is off-limits, but also any place near Zhabei within the Japanese military's sphere of influence. Avoid being coerced and humiliated by traitors.

The other day, a telegram from Shenyang reported that Gu Weijun's staff, Ge Gongzhen, and six or seven others, were surrounded and arrested by pseudo-state military police when they entered Shenyang city to investigate the situation. Although nominally pseudo-state military police, it goes without saying who commands these pseudo-state military police. Therefore, Chinese people cannot go to the Northeast, just as our good people cannot go to Zhabei.

The League of Nations' dispatch of an investigation team to inspect the Northeast was originally a ridiculous and perfunctory move. Zhang Xueliang consistently embraced a policy of non-resistance, and there were originally no traces of war in the Northeast. The puppet show of the bogus Manchukuo is known by everyone as a trick to deceive. What is the investigation team going to investigate?

Science

Thermos Bottle 167

— Zhou Ruichuan

People in the past often thought about how to keep the temperature of the water we use. Scientists also often thought about how to preserve liquefied gases for several hours. Because when you turn a gas into a liquid, if you don't find a way to preserve it, it will continue to evaporate due to the external temperature and become a gas again, because it is in a gaseous state at room temperature. For example, oxygen, nitrogen, and hydrogen are all in a gaseous state at room temperature. Since James Dewar (1842-1923), a Scottish scientist, invented the vacuum flask, this type of bottle that can keep warm (what we commonly call a thermos bottle) has been successful. The principle is to use a double-walled glass bottle (an inner layer and an outer layer) and completely extract the air in between using a pump, which creates a vacuum. If you put hot water in, the incoming and outgoing forces of convection and conduction of heat, except for a slight amount at the stopper, are nowhere to be found on the entire bottle. The inner layer of the outer wall and the outer layer of the inner wall are coated with mercury, so that its function is like a mirror, which can reflect the radiation falling on it. Heat is only transmitted by conduction, convection, and radiation as methods of heat transfer, so all three are separated from the external temperature, so the contents of this bottle can maintain its temperature for a long time. If you put liquefied gas - the temperature of this liquefied gas is always below minus one hundred degrees Celsius - or cold things in, its temperature is also insulated from the outside world, so it can also maintain its temperature for a long time.

A Glimpse of Edward Road (East-West-North-South) 168

— Hongshui

It was late, and the bright lights of light red and light green illuminated the scenery near "The Great World" as if it were daytime. Under the towering Western-style buildings, hundreds and thousands of people were crowded together, men, women, old, and young. Most of their faces were filled with joyful expressions, and they seemed to be lingering and wandering there.

"Buicks" and "Dodges," brightly colored cars, one after another, sped along the smooth and flat Edward Road. In the "Pa...pa..." sounds, it seemed like the wealthy merchants, gentlemen, ladies, and misses in "Motorcade" were saying triumphantly, "This is our blessing!"

The adjacent rows of cinemas, coffee shops, and dance halls enticed many fashionable couples; whispering sweet nothings, they ran inside in pairs to spend their entire evening, pursuing and indulging.

The red and green girls on the side of the road, living in the eighteenth hell, reluctantly created artificial "curves," displaying themselves in rows and groups with graceful and coquettish postures, in order to win the favor of those who seek flowers and willows, following them like flies chasing after something stinking and rank.

"Mountain Hermit of Crouching Clouds" and "Taoist of Mount Lu," countless fortune-tellers, each had one or two old women and three or four poor friends publicly on their stands, their eyes fixed on the glass plate that said, "No charge for the poor, no empty talk," under the dim kerosene lamp. They kept grumbling and asking: What is meant by "the father dies before the mother"? What is meant by "wearing my nose, eating my ears"?

In the corners of the alleys, there were people who played games of chance; shouting in an awful voice: "Press quickly, press quickly, it will open immediately..." Some would laugh heartily; while others would be wooden.

Wealthy people who had just returned from a drunken feast at the ×× Palace inevitably encountered beggars dressed in tattered clothes, following them and offering blessings in exchange for money...

If you don't know what Shanghai is really like, then you just need to run to "The Great World" and look around, and you will instantly see a true portrayal. Everything seems to be depicting the concrete epitome of the word "evil." Although on the other hand, you can also see the convenience of transportation and the development of culture, it always feels that "the flaws outweigh the merits."

How Sad

Scars of Life 169

— Yan Meng

Like an era of blood in the storms, wandering and drifting east, west, north, and south, like a flower detached from its branch, dried duckweed, fallen leaves. At the beginning of entering the world, harboring a full of enthusiasm, naturally, it is inevitable to complain and lament in the quiet deep night, and even drop pointless tears. Now, after being nurtured by unhealthy worldliness and experiencing the wind and frost of the human world, the tender buds of the soul have long been destroyed. Besides shuffling along the muddy streets, the life tasted is as ethereal as smoke, as unfounded as a dream.

The years urge old age, the sorrow of the old country, the oppression of life, lingering and nostalgic youth is fading, tender attempts, splendid dreams, only replaced by scars of food and clothing on the forehead. The most unsuitable for the life of a big city, the most unable to settle in the snobbish streets, and yet precisely in that big city made up of shame and sin, eking out a living as a fallen person.

Because the ambitions have not yet achieved even a small success, I am unwilling to be destroyed. As a result of striving for survival, after delving deep into the core of society, I realize that reactionary authorities in the world are easily tempted by utilitarianism. Therefore, everyone is conquered, bowing their heads and saying to the evil forces: "I surrender." Entering society is like leaving a pure and bright paradise. Young people, save yourselves quickly! Maintain your sincere and enlightened hearts and beware of the traps in the darkness.

For the sake of the unknowable future, hope is guiding us forward, giving us the heat and all the stimulation, just like the thorns beside the rose. However, the birds welcoming the spring are praising and singing. Living with tearful eyes, I originally wanted to explore the mystery and ultimate truth of life, but everything is shattered, demons occupy heaven, leaving us pure people in the cellar, they are still cursing. Friends, we are as tame as sheep, which is what constitutes the "good people" of sin! Why not raise our arms and shout: "Effort!"

Joke

Big and Small Newspaper Headlines 170

— Gou

Yesterday, the local supplement's newspaper heading had two - one big and one small. The typesetting gentlemen certainly overlooked it, but the gentlemen who proofread the proofs were also inevitably careless, creating such a joke. Please, gentlemen readers, don't misunderstand and add one more because it looks good.

Zhu Zili, the central minister of the Qing Dynasty, had high cheekbones, a long beard, and many schemes, and was known as a double-material Cao Cao. In Peking opera, there are also double-package cases, and dramas with plays within plays, and riddle transmissions, etc. Now, there are two newspaper headings. Could it be that they are as good-looking as plays within plays?

No - no - definitely not - officials like to have as many concubines as possible, and wealthy merchants like to accumulate more and more gold and banknotes. Our local supplement actually learned to be aristocratic yesterday and took a concubine.

Someone said, good - according to what you said, please add one more tomorrow, or simply add a few more small newspaper headings. Wouldn't that be even more aristocratic?

I said no - more money means more people trying to help and getting busy, and more concubines means more waves of jealousy. I will never dare to take a concubine again in the future, haha!

A Scale and a Claw

Zhabei Now 171

— Xigang

Yesterday, a friend came from Zhabei and said that Zhabei now is somewhat different from Zhabei when the artillery was booming and the fire was blazing! Now, it is full of peaceful scenes? Even though those guys with eight whiskers and chanting "Ge Da, Ge Da" are still strutting around!

In the past (since January 28th), on the streets of Zhabei, what the eyes saw were only kind people with faces full of grief and indignation, crying men, women, old, and young. What about now? Now, there are hordes of opium addicts, piles of gamblers, and groups of prostitutes appearing on the streets!

They have smiles on their faces, as if they are saying: "Fortunately, someone came to patronize this time, otherwise, we would never have a chance to make a name for ourselves"?

Indeed, Zhabei is peaceful after all, and the businesses of "opium," "gambling," and "prostitution" are particularly prosperous. They are living a happy (?) spring life!

The summer is coming soon, and epidemics of various diseases are likely to run rampant. The so-called great war must be followed by a great epidemic. In view of this, the pharmacy has been pained to offer a special discount in order to reach a wide audience. Therefore, since the big discount started on the 15th of this month, the shop has been extremely crowded. During the discount period, celebrity perfume essence is also available as a gift.

Shanghai First Special District District Court Notice 173

Notice is hereby given that, in order to facilitate litigants in inquiring about all litigation procedures, this court has established an information office within the court from May 1st and has formulated rules for compliance. In the future, if litigants have any unclear matters, they may inquire at the information office at any time in accordance with the scope specified in these rules to avoid misunderstandings. This notice is hereby issued to all litigants for their information. President Zhou Xianjue ▲ Information Office Rules 1. This court has established an information office with one clerk in charge to facilitate inquiries by litigants. 2. Litigants may inquire at the information office at any time regarding unclear matters concerning the purchase of forms, submission of forms, payment of fees, copying, registration, and other matters related to the progress of the litigation. 3. The information office shall immediately answer the inquiries of litigants in detail. If there are any unclear matters, the information office may instruct litigants to write down the reasons in the inquiry register or write them down on their behalf and answer them after verification. 4. The information office shall provide detailed guidance on the inquiries of litigants and shall not engage in deception, obstruction, or demands for payment. 5. Litigants should only inquire about the matters specified in Article 2 and should not involve other matters. Otherwise, no answers will be given.

(1) Notice of Auction: This court, in the case of creditor Shen Hexiang versus debtor Xu Wenrong regarding a deposit dispute, has seized and appraised the debtor's property listed below. The auction date is hereby set for 4:00 PM on May 2nd, and the auction will be conducted by a clerk of this court directing a bailiff in conjunction with a bailiff. Residents who wish to purchase the property should immediately report to the bailiff's office of this court in order to be led to the location for viewing and then bid on schedule. If there are two or more bidders, the bidder with the highest price will be the buyer, and the auctioned property will be given to the buyer upon payment of the full price on the spot. Shanghai First Special District Local Court 175

First Criminal Judgment: The General Inspectorate vs. Lu Chunsheng Embezzlement Case (Main Text) Lu Chunsheng is fined 14 yuan for embezzlement of lost property. If the fine is not paid in full, he will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined will be offset against the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. The Putuo Police Station vs. Hu Chengxian et al. Gambling Case (Main Text) Hu Chengxian and Li Yuanren are each fined ten yuan for joint gambling. If the fines are not paid in full, they will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The gambling paraphernalia and funds are confiscated. The Xinzha Police Station vs. Xu Guozhen Injury Case (Main Text) This case is not accepted. The Hongkou Police Station vs. Chen Zhang Theft Case (Main Text) Chen Zhang is sentenced to six months imprisonment for theft. The Huishan Police Station vs. Li Dehe et al. Embezzlement Case (Main Text) Li Dehe and Lu Chunmei are each fined twenty yuan for embezzlement of lost property. If the fines are not paid in full, they will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The General Inspectorate vs. Zhang Xiaobao Theft Case (Main Text) Zhang Xiaobao is found not guilty, but should be sent to a reformatory for one month of moral education. The Laozha Police Station vs. Ning Qian Gui Opium Case (Main Text) Ning Qiangui is fined thirty yuan for possession of opium. If the fine is not paid in full, he will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. One tael of opium is confiscated. The Laozha Police Station vs. Chen Huiqing Opium Case (Main Text) Chen Huiqing is fined forty yuan for possession of opium. If the fine is not paid in full, he will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. One tael and two qian of opium are confiscated. The Xinzha Police Station vs. Ding Congsan Embezzlement Case (Main Text) Ding Congsan is sentenced to three months imprisonment for embezzlement. The Huisi Police Station vs. Qin Ahu's Use of Counterfeit Banknotes Case (Main Text) Qin Ahu is sentenced to five years imprisonment for using counterfeit General Bank banknotes. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined will be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two hundred days. Five ten-yuan notes of the counterfeit Bank of China and three ten-yuan notes of the counterfeit Banque Franco-Chinoise are confiscated. The Laozha Police Station vs. Zhu Hailan Fraud Case (Main Text) Zhu Hailan is sentenced to one year imprisonment for fraud. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined will be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. The portion of the related civil lawsuit is transferred to the Civil Division of this court for trial. The General Inspectorate vs. Yang Zhizhu Embezzlement Case (Main Text) Yang Zhizhu is sentenced to one year imprisonment for embezzlement of objects held in his business capacity. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined will be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. Sentence suspended for three years. Embezzlement Case (Main Text) Shen Erlang, Shen Qixiang, and Yu Sanlang are each sentenced to four months imprisonment for jointly and continuously embezzling the property of others. The part of the bill of lading concerning the alteration is confiscated. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined will be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined will be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. First Instance Civil Judgment: 1. Mei Yi Co., Ltd. vs. Lu Caisi Gai et al. for Goods Payment Case (Main Text) The defendant Lu Caisi Gai shall repay the plaintiff silver 10,507 taels and 5 qian. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Lu Caisi Gai. The remainder of the plaintiff's claims is rejected. 2. Sun Bo Ji Accounting Firm, namely Sun Bosheng, vs. Defendant Sihai Shenglou Chen Songquan for Eviction, Rent Payment, and Return of Transfer Fee, Counter-Suit Case (Main Text) The defendant shall vacate the rented premises located at M50 to 157, 165½, 166½, 167½, 142, and 164½ Fuzhou Road in this city and return them to the plaintiff for repossession. The defendant shall pay rent of silver 510 taels per month from December 9, 1931, until the date of eviction. The plaintiff shall return the defendant's transfer fee of silver 3,250 taels. The aforementioned rent and transfer fee shall be offset against each other. The remainder of the plaintiff's claims and its request for provisional execution, as well as the remainder of the defendant's counter-suit, are all rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by both parties. 3. Qiu Dinglai vs. Mao Yongchang Installment Payment Case (Main Text) The defendant in this lawsuit, Mao Yongchang, shall repay the plaintiff in this lawsuit, Qiu Dinglai, silver 2,550 taels, plus statutory late payment interest at an annual rate of 5% from the due date until the date of execution. The counter-claim of the counter-plaintiff is rejected. The litigation costs of this lawsuit and the counter-suit shall be borne by Mao Yongchang. 4. Bi Xinsheng vs. Xu Quansheng Debt Case (Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff six hundred yuan on behalf of Tong Zhaojin. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. 5. Su Jiaxin vs. Gu Rongrong et al. Debt Case (Main Text) The defendant Gu Rongrong shall repay the plaintiff eight hundred yuan. This amount shall be repaid in monthly installments of fifty yuan until paid in full. If it cannot be repaid in full, the defendant Yao Zhijiang shall be responsible for the repayment. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Gu Rongrong. 6. Lun Sheng vs. Zhu Guanlin et al. Debt Case (Main Text) The defendants shall jointly and severally repay the plaintiff two hundred and ninety yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne jointly and severally by the defendants. 7. A Mo Sheng vs. Yang Baomei Debt Case (Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff one hundred and twenty yuan. This amount shall be repaid in monthly installments of ten yuan until paid in full. The remainder of the plaintiff's claims is rejected. The plaintiff shall bear 1/10 of the litigation costs, and the defendant shall bear 89/100. 8. Ou Changle vs. Liu Jishan Rent Arrears and Eviction Case (Main Text) The application is rejected. The application costs shall be borne by the applicant. 9. Gongyi Accounting Firm Xie Shenru vs. Xinxin Company Store Owner Cao Liangui Rent Arrears and Eviction Case (Main Text) The defendant shall immediately vacate the premises and pay the plaintiff rent of 175 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. 10. Le Li Shi vs. Wang Fulin et al. Debt Case (Main Text) The plaintiff's claims are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

Criminal Judgment: Police Department vs. Shen Youji Embezzlement Case (Main Text) Shen Youji, with the intention of illegal possession for himself, embezzled property no longer in the possession of its owner, is fined sixty yuan. If he does not pay the fine in full, he may commute the penalty to imprisonment, with two yuan equal to one day of imprisonment. Days spent in detention before sentencing may be credited against the fine at the rate of one day for two yuan. Police Department vs. Li Ruliang Embezzlement Case (Main Text) Li Ruliang, with the intention of illegal possession for himself, embezzled property no longer in the possession of its owner, is fined one hundred yuan. If he does not pay the fine in full, he may commute the penalty to imprisonment, with two yuan equal to one day of imprisonment. Days spent in detention before sentencing may be credited against the fine at the rate of one day for two yuan. Police Department vs. Pan Junsheng Obstructing Official Business Case (Main Text) Pan Junsheng, who used violence and coercion against a public official lawfully performing his duties, is sentenced to two months imprisonment. Days spent in detention before sentencing may be credited against the imprisonment at the rate of two days for one day. Police Department vs. Chen Dezi Theft Case (Main Text) Chen Dezi, who damaged a door and committed theft, is sentenced to six months imprisonment. Days spent in detention before sentencing may be credited against the imprisonment at the rate of two days for one day. Police Department vs. Jin Yangshi et al. Interference with Marriage Case (Main Text) Public prosecution in this case is not accepted. Police Department vs. Wang Jinrong et al. Opium Case (Main Text) Wang Jinrong, who provided premises for others to smoke opium substitutes, is sentenced to six months imprisonment. Ying Linfa and Hu Yousheng, who smoked opium substitutes, are each sentenced to one month imprisonment. Days spent in detention before sentencing may be credited against the imprisonment at the rate of two days for one day. Ying Linfa's sentence is suspended for two years. Two opium pipes and four hundred and forty red pills are confiscated and destroyed according to the list. Police Department vs. Wang Yuantai et al. Opium Case (Main Text) Wang Yuantai, who provided premises for others to smoke opium substitutes, is sentenced to six months imprisonment. Theft Case (Main Text) Xing Juntao, who is a habitual thief, is sentenced to one year and two months imprisonment. Wu Yuru, who concealed stolen goods, is sentenced to thirty days detention. Days spent in detention before sentencing may be credited against the imprisonment or detention at the rate of two days for one day. One pair of pliers, three short chisels, and eighteen keys are all confiscated. Police Department vs. Song Rufu et al. Robbery Case (Main Text) Song Rufu and Chen Deming, who formed a gang of three or more persons and robbed the property of others, are each sentenced to one year and six months imprisonment. Days spent in detention before sentencing may be credited against the imprisonment at the rate of two days for one day.
